## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start]) --> ParseArgs[Parse Command Line Arguments]
    ParseArgs --> InitSpark[Initialize SparkContext with YARN]
    InitSpark --> ConfigSpark[Configure Spark Settings]
    ConfigSpark --> CreateSQL[Create SQLContext]
    CreateSQL --> ReadMaxID[Read max_id from PostgreSQL table]
    ReadMaxID --> CheckMaxID{Max ID Retrieved?}
    CheckMaxID -->|Success| UseMaxID[Use Retrieved max_id]
    CheckMaxID -->|Error| DefaultID[Use Default max_id = 6000000000]
    UseMaxID --> ReadTable[Read Full Table from PostgreSQL]
    DefaultID --> ReadTable
    ReadTable --> ConfigPartitions[Configure Partitions & Fetch Size]
    ConfigPartitions --> LoadData[Load Data with JDBC]
    LoadData --> GetLatestPath[Calculate Latest Path]
    GetLatestPath --> TryReadLatest{Try Read Latest Parquet}
    TryReadLatest -->|Success| SetLatestDF[Set latest_df]
    TryReadLatest -->|Exception| NullLatest[latest_df = None]
    SetLatestDF --> WriteParquet[Write DataFrame to S3 as Parquet]
    NullLatest --> WriteParquet
    WriteParquet --> ReadBack[Read Back Written Parquet]
    ReadBack --> WriteLatest[Write to Latest Path]
    WriteLatest --> End([End])
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main
    participant SparkContext
    participant SQLContext
    participant PostgreSQL
    participant S3
    
    Main->>Main: Parse sys.argv for DB credentials
    Main->>SparkContext: Initialize with master=yarn
    SparkContext->>SparkContext: Configure timeouts & settings
    Main->>SQLContext: Create SQLContext(sc)
    Main->>SQLContext: Read format=jdbc
    SQLContext->>PostgreSQL: SELECT max(id) FROM table
    PostgreSQL-->>SQLContext: Return max_id
    alt max_id retrieval fails
        Main->>Main: Set max_id = 6000000000
    end
    Main->>SQLContext: Read table with partitioning
    SQLContext->>PostgreSQL: Query table with 1000 partitions
    PostgreSQL-->>SQLContext: Return DataFrame
    Main->>Main: get_latest_path(s3_output_path)
    Main->>SQLContext: Try read latest parquet
    SQLContext->>S3: Read latest_path
    alt latest exists
        S3-->>SQLContext: Return latest_df
    else exception
        Main->>Main: latest_df = None
    end
    Main->>SQLContext: df.write.parquet(s3_output_path)
    SQLContext->>S3: Write parquet (overwrite mode)
    Main->>SQLContext: Read back parquet
    SQLContext->>S3: Read s3_output_path
    S3-->>SQLContext: Return DataFrame
    Main->>SQLContext: df.write.parquet(latest_path)
    SQLContext->>S3: Write latest parquet (overwrite mode)
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initializing
    Initializing --> ConfiguringDB: Parse Arguments
    ConfiguringDB --> InitializingSpark: DB Config Ready
    InitializingSpark --> SparkConfigured: SparkContext Created
    SparkConfigured --> ReadingMaxID: SQLContext Ready
    ReadingMaxID --> MaxIDRetrieved: Query Success
    ReadingMaxID --> MaxIDDefaulted: Query Failed
    MaxIDRetrieved --> LoadingTable
    MaxIDDefaulted --> LoadingTable
    LoadingTable --> DataLoaded: JDBC Read Complete
    DataLoaded --> CheckingLatest: Calculate Paths
    CheckingLatest --> WritingData: Latest Check Done
    WritingData --> ReadingBack: Parquet Written
    ReadingBack --> UpdatingLatest: Data Read
    UpdatingLatest --> [*]: Latest Updated
```
